<h1 class="firstHeading" id="firstHeading" lang="en">1983–84 UEFA Cup</h1>
<div class="mw-body-content" id="bodyContent">

<p>The <b>1983–84 <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/UEFA_Cup" title="UEFA Cup">UEFA Cup</a></b> was won by <a href="/wiki/Tottenham_Hotspur_F.C." title="Tottenham Hotspur F.C.">Tottenham Hotspur</a> on penalties over <a href="/wiki/R.S.C._Anderlecht" title="R.S.C. Anderlecht">Anderlecht</a>.</p>
<p></p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Association_ranking">Association ranking</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=1983%E2%80%9384_UEFA_Cup&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: Association ranking">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>For the 1983–84 UEFA Cup, the associations are allocated places according to their 1982 <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/UEFA_country_coefficient" title="UEFA country coefficient">UEFA country coefficients</a>, which takes into account their performance in European competitions from 1977–78 to 1981–82.</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Teams">Teams</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=1983%E2%80%9384_UEFA_Cup&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Teams">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>The labels in the parentheses show how each team qualified for competition:</p>
<ul>
<li>TH: Title holders</li>
<li>CW: Cup winners</li>
<li>CR: Cup runners-up</li>
<li>LC: League Cup winners</li>
<li>2nd, 3rd, 4th, 5th, 6th, etc.: League position</li>
<li>P-W: End-of-season European competition play-offs winners</li>
</ul>

Anderlecht">Anderlecht</a></b></td>
<td style="text-align: center;">2–0 (<a class="external text" href="http://www.uefa.com/uefaeuropaleague/season=1983/matches/round=585/match=1114/postmatch/lineups/index.html" rel="nofollow">Report</a>)</td>
<td style="text-align: center;">0–3 (<a class="external text" href="http://www.uefa.com/uefaeuropaleague/season=1983/matches/round=585/match=1115/postmatch/lineups/index.html" rel="nofollow">Report</a>)</td>
</tr>
</table>
<p>In 1997, it was revealed that the chairman of Anderlecht had paid a bribe worth £27,000 to the referee to help fix the result of the second-leg of their semi-final. <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Indy_bribe_1-0"><a href="#cite_note-Indy_bribe-1">[1]</a></sup> During the match, Anderlecht were awarded a dubious <a href="/wiki/Penalty_kick_(association_football)" title="Penalty kick (association football)">penalty</a>, and a Nottingham Forest goal in the last minute - that would have won them the tie on the <a href="/wiki/Away_goals_rule" title="Away goals rule">away goals rule</a> - was disallowed.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-2"><a href="#cite_note-2">[2]</a></sup> In 2016 it emerged that UEFA had known about the bribe since 1993 but had taken no action until the information was made public in 1997, <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-3"><a href="#cite_note-3">[3]</a></sup> when UEFA suspended Anderlecht from the next European tournament for which they qualified. <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Indy_bribe_1-1"><a href="#cite_note-Indy_bribe-1">[1]</a></sup> On qualifying for the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/1998-99_UEFA_Cup" title="1998-99 UEFA Cup">1998-99 UEFA Cup</a>, Anderlecht appealed the suspension in the <a href="/wiki/Court_of_Arbitration_for_Sport" title="Court of Arbitration for Sport">Court of Arbitration for Sport</a>, which overturned the ban on the grounds that it was made by UEFA's Executive Committee, which did not have the authority to issue the ban. <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-4"><a href="#cite_note-4">[4]</a></sup></p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="First_leg_5">First leg</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=1983%E2%80%9384_UEFA_Cup&amp;action=edit&amp;section=16" title="Edit section: First leg">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Second_leg_5">Second leg</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=1983%E2%80%9384_UEFA_Cup&amp;action=edit&amp;section=17" title="Edit section: Second leg">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
